local drive that provides files or data to be uploaded to other drives or receives files downloaded from other drives.\r\n\r\n\r\nTASK: \r\nA 'task' is a collection of sources with a target drive, through which a sync, backup or restore operation can be performed.\r\n\r\n\r\nThe app can perform:\r\n\r\n* FULL SYNC: compares and synchronises files at two locations, deleted files in one location are deleted at the other, while new files at one location are uploaded to the other\r\n\r\n* BACKUP SYNC: upload changed files from sources to the destination drive\r\n\r\n* RESTORE SYNC: download changed files on a drive to target sources\r\n\r\n* FILE MANAGER: list and browse files and folders on a drive, upload or download files to and from a drive, delete/rename files and folders on a drive.\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nUsage:\r\nFile transfers are performed in tasks and you can create as many tasks for any drive, and with as many sources as you prefer.\r\n\r\n\r\nWhen you create a task, you will  \r\n1. add a list of sources that point to the data you want to backup or restore. For files, this will be the folder containing the files. \r\n\r\n2. add a destination drive and then select a destination folder on the drive where the data will be uploaded to or downloaded from.\r\n\r\n\r\nEach source in a task can have a 'path'. A source path is a folder name, relative to the current task's drive destination folder ,\r\nwhere a source's files are uploaded to during a backup or downloaded from during
